It honestly baffles me how this store has 4 stars. I ordered the other night; a simple cheese bread and deep dish pizza with a few sauces on the side. When the driver shows up, he doesn't have my cheese bread. He tells me that it's no problem, he'll call the store and have it delivered.

After waiting another 20 minutes, I call to check on the status of it. The driver NEVER CALLED THE DAMN STORE! So I speak to the manager, she takes care of me and for the trouble she asks what kind of 2-Liter I want. I tell her Coke and feel good...for a moment.

Finally, when my cheese bread showed up, the driver handed it to me, expecting a tip and throwing an attitude at me because I already gave it to the driver the screwed up in the first place. Whatever, I sit down to realize they sent me a BOTTLE of Coke, NOT a 2-Liter. Really? Why would you say one thing and do another? Are these people high? I open up my bag of sauces and lo and behold, it was the wrong damn sauces.

I've worked in a local pizza shop FAR less equipped than a chain store like this and we would put them to shame with how poorly and  sad this store is run. I will be doing everything I can to never order here again, nor have anyone I know order from here again.<//text>

< review>
We have been looking for a good breakfast place and decided to try Country Skillets in Ripon. This place did not disappoint. The food was very fresh, tasty and the portions were good size. The wait staff was very friendly and attentive.

My wife had the Farmers Country Skillet. I was told it was tasty and there was plenty of food. The Biscuit was really good. It was served with a side of gravy. Nice flavor for the gravy. I had the Denver Omelette with Country Potatoes. I wish the potatoes had a little more seasoning (just my preference). We will definitely come back here again.

It can get a little noisy but that is ok. Don‚Äôt come here expecting a quiet environment. It is located close to the sports park so there are large groups that show up between games.<//review>

< Review>
My two boys had been going to Dental Fun Zone for years, we were always fairly satisfied with the care they received. The staff was kind, friendly and helpful and the dental assistants whom performed the cleaning were always wonderful. The dentists were, let's just say, okay. My complaint is about the orthodontist and the communication regarding my son's braces. During our initial consult with the orthodontist, he spent maybe two minutes with my son and I. His assistant spent the next 30 min. discussing cost and answering any questions I had. After the consultation I asked if we could take the estimate home to talk over with my husband. Our family had tentative plans to move out of LA, and it was explained to me by the orthodontist's assistant that my son would have to absolutely see the same orthodontist for each follow up appointment and for the braces to be removed. Since it was explained to me that my son would need them on for two years I was nervous to commit if we moved. She said the estimate was good for 30-plus days. Once we decided to go forth with Dental Fun Zone for his braces I tried weekly to get in touch with the orthodontist or his assistant, but they never returned my call! I even went into the office twice and the front desk said they would deliver the message, and still no call back. After being brushed off for so long we decided not to return to Dental Fun Zone for regular check-ups, and to take our money elsewhere for braces. Very annoyed.< /Review>

< review>
We chose this dentist based on reviews and what a mistake.  If you are a PPO patient, perhaps this is the place of childhood dental dreams the reviews purport, but as a DMO patient we were herded in on the ONE day a week that CERTAIN doctors see DMO patients.  My 12 yr old, who has been seeing a dentist and having dental work (cleanings, fillings and extractions) since he was 9 months old with NO ISSUES, never so much as a complaint that he didn't want to return to the dentist or that something hurt or was scary, came out of this exam room in tears.  He was in agony after a CLEANING, a boy who does not cry was sobbing in pain from a CLEANING.  They proceeded to tell us he had 2 cavities that needed filling and recommended Nitrous because was very apprehensive during his cleaning.  It took them 3 months to get back to us to let us know that the DMO denied coverages for the fillings and "oh by the way" it's actually 3 fillings and he also needs sealants.  The required work kept increasing with the price tag.  I was clearly NOT returning to this office and sought a second opinion.  A second opinion that I paid cash for, after reviewing the X-rays and a full exam they determined he had no cavities, but some pitting in previous sealants.  10 minutes, no novocaine or nitrous and she fixed the sealants.

We were DMO patients only due to an error in paperwork when my husband started a new job and are fortunate to have the means to seek a second opinion and the wherewithal to ask questions and push for answers because the billing and treatment practices at Children's Dental FunZone are suspect at best.<//review>

Sorry.  I really can't give it more than one star.

My son's medical insurance directed me to the Children's Dental Funzone.  The office is clean.  Appointments are usually 30-45 minutes late but usually not more than 1 hour.  Dentists seem professional and good with children.

So why only 1 star?

I really want to like this place but I can't.  Front desk staff are SO frustrating to deal with.  Junior staff are condescending and passive aggressive.  Office manager (Anna) is friendly but talking to her is like going around in circles.

They wanted approx $3,000 for a course of treatment with my child.  When I asked for details I was told that he would need to come in every 6-8 weeks.  I asked if we could book those appointments in advance.  They said no, but rather than give a straight answer, I got 5000 different (contradictory) reasons why this would be bad for me to do and result in worse care for my son.  (See end of this message for examples)

The staff person even tried to tell me that the clinic had never (!) had a case where someone was trying to make an appointment within the stated time from by couldn't.  This was pretty shocking because it has happened to me a few times already -- virtually every!  I had to wait 4 months once for the next check up time for my son (in addition to the standard 6 months in between checkups).

I asked what happens in a scenario where I pay all this money, the clinic takes my money, the clinic puts all of this equipment in my little boy's mouth that needs to be maintained and serviced on a regular basis (6-8 weeks) but their next available appointment is in their usual 4-5 months.  She didn't have any answer for that.

I really don't think a clinic should be marketing medical services for children if they can't be sure that they will be able to perform those services according to their own safety guidelines.  I am really bothered by the fact that this doesn't seem to bother anyone at Children's Dental Funzone and that, after having laid this out, they were still trying to market these $ervices to my family.

----

EXAMPLES OF THE DIFFERENT BS REASONS WHY THEY WON'T MAKE APPOINTMENTS IN ADVANCE

CDFZ Staff: "We don't make appointments in advance because even though almost all of them are scheduled for the same length of time every once in a while like if your son breaks the equipment, we'd need to schedule a longer appointment and then your son would fall behind?"

Me: "Why would he fall behind?  In the remote possibility that he breaks the equipment, I would have to call on that day and make a longer appointment anyway and be at the mercy of whatever is available.  That's no different than if I didn't have any appointments set up.  So in the extreme case, I'm no worse than when we started but in 99% of situations we'd be ahead"

CDFZ Staff: "Ummmm....  well we don't like to do that because it makes scheduling complicated"

Me:  "What is complicated about booking in advance?  If he needs 4 sessions every 6-8 weeks why not book them now?  What is complicated about that?"

CDFZ Staff: "It's because of patient care"

Me:  "What is better about patient care if you put a ton of medical equipment in my son's mouth, cash my check, and then are too busy to see him again?"

CDFZ Staff: "But if you son breaks the equipment then he would need a longer appointment"

Me: "Yes, we just covered that at the beginning of this conversation..." [and we cycle through various 'reasons' again]</Review>
